Essays

Talking About the Pen Industry 200

— (Ning Ziqiang)

——We want to promote small industries——

The writing brush is an object for promoting domestic goods. The rise and fall of the brush industry is of great importance to the future of domestic goods. After the economic downturn enveloped the country, the common people after the disaster almost became fish in a dried-up ditch, and those in charge of the pen industry could not but be affected by it.

The raw materials for writing brushes are hemp and animal hair. Hemp is purchased from Jiangxi and Anhui provinces, costing at least 20 cents per pound. Animal hair is purchased from Xuzhou, with each basket weighing about 1.5 pounds and costing about 5 yuan. Brush handles are purchased from the southern Anhui area, costing about one copper coin per piece. Then, with the addition of labor, washing, brushing, and manufacturing, a skilled worker can produce 30 brushes per day, with a salary of about 10 yuan.

Based on this, the cost of labor and raw materials is so high that a writing brush cannot be profitable unless it costs 40 cents. However, since general purchasing power is now below the baseline, even if pen merchants sell at reduced prices, they still cannot sell, let alone maintain costs!

Firing Pottery 201

— Tian Sheweng

Firing pottery is an industry that we invented long ago, along with papermaking, winemaking, etc. It has nothing to do with science or lack thereof, and it has already achieved considerable success. In a village, as long as someone advocates these small industries, there will be no idle people, no abandoned land, and the country will not have to worry about not being rich and strong.

The × village along the Yao River is backed by mountains and faces water, with very beautiful scenery. The villagers all make a living by burning pottery. They work at sunrise and rest at sunset, living their lives steadily. However, firstly, due to the nature of the soil, and secondly, due to adhering to old methods and not seeking progress, they can only burn some bricks and tiles, which are not as good as the products of Jingdezhen, Jiangxi. It is said that people in Fenghua can also make paper, but the products are not very good either; these are all the responsibilities of the local "intellectual class" and "propertied class"!

If the pottery kiln is not wide enough, Xue Pinggui and Wang Baochuan could not have lived there as a couple. Just taking the brick kiln as an example, it can probably fire 65,000 bricks per kiln. The capital is really small, probably requiring 50 to 60 yuan worth of pine firewood, which is enough, but labor accounts for most of it.

Digging up river mud, treading it with feet to make it tough, rotten and uniform, then putting the mud in a mold, drying it, dumping it out, and piling it in the kiln, then it can be fired. Pine firewood is put into the kiln door, and the raging fire melts and burns the entire kiln. After burning continuously for a day and night, iron wire mesh, rice straw, fine sand and other things are used to seal the kiln opening, and water is introduced from the kiln opening - according to insiders, 60 loads of water are required per kiln. - The water flows into the kiln and spreads like rain, so that the fired bricks gradually cool down. On the third day, when the kiln door is opened, it is still very warm inside, and the fired bricks are transported out, and they can be applied.

This is the most convenient old method of firing pottery kilns. Although it has not yet been eliminated, I think that the survival of the fittest is a natural law, and rapid improvement is necessary! This is not just about firing pottery kilns.

In the place where pottery kilns are fired, you can't find a single woman; because the kiln workers often work naked, naturally women avoid it. This is also a bad habit that should be eradicated.

Self-Spinning Wool Yarn 202

— Yan Boge

There are so many unemployed people in society, and it is too cruel to just watch them suffer from the pain of freezing and starvation due to unemployment without thinking of ways to help them. Like modern China, it is precisely necessary to promote small industries, and the raw materials are best local products.

Wool yarn has a wide range of uses, and the raw material is sheep's wool, which everyone knows. In the past, wool yarn was all supplied by foreign countries, because we didn't know the secret of spinning wool yarn, but it is actually very easy.

The farmers in the Changxing (Zhejiang Province) area like to raise sheep the most, and almost every household raises ten or so sheep. In addition to farming for a living, the farmers here also engage in sericulture and raising sheep as side businesses, but silkworms are not raised in the summer and autumn seasons. The mulberry leaves are left to grow on the tree branches, and after a severe frost, they are picked and fed to the sheep. The sheep's dung and urine can also fertilize the fields, which is actually a very good method of circular production!

Sheep are very fertile, and every winter, many farmers are idle at home with nothing to do, so they lead their sheep to nearby towns and villages to do slaughtering and meat selling business. However, there is a lot of wool scraped off, and now they have learned the method of spinning yarn with wool, so recently rural women have been spinning yarn themselves. The method is to take a certain amount of wool and stone alkali shavings, add boiling water to soak, then rinse with clean water, dry in the sun, and dye it at will. The spinning procedure uses old-fashioned cotton spinning equipment. Although the method is very clumsy, it is a good way to promote local small industries for women to take this as a pastime when they have nothing to do, and I hope everyone will experiment with it!

— Hong

Yixing Pottery 203

— Hua Ling

There is a very harsh saying in the area of Suzhou, called "Three coppers for a pair of Yixing chamber pots," meaning "only good at talking," describing people who can only talk but cannot do things. Although this saying has no deep meaning, "Yixing Pottery" does have a value worth mentioning.

The production centers of Yixing pottery are Shushan and Dingshan towns, located southeast of Yixing city. Shushan mainly produces teapots and teacups, while Dingshan produces a large number of bowls and dishes. However, this is not an absolute restriction, as Shushan kilns also manufacture and sell bowls and dishes, and Dingshan potters also make tea sets. It's just that these two areas have different main sales channels, hence this distinction.

Among the residents centered around Shushan and Dingshan, at least nine out of ten families rely on the pottery industry for a living. Although agriculture is also quite developed in these two areas, it is clearly in a secondary position. Children raised in the pottery area are able to mold various pottery prototypes around the age of ten. Indeed, the pottery industry in Yixing has a history of two thousand years, and the potters rely on the inexhaustible clay for their livelihood, which can be said to be a gift from nature.

From the Kangxi period until around the tenth year of the Republic of China, it was the golden age of Yixing pottery. It was not only popular throughout the country, but also welcomed everywhere in Japan and Southeast Asia. Even upper-class families in Europe and America had a set of Chinese-made Yixing tea sets or dish toys. During the early Republic of China and late Qing Dynasty, the average annual export value of pottery from Shushan and Dingshan was about two million to two and a half million yuan. However, in recent years, under the pressure of foreign porcelain, enamel, and glassware, it has gradually declined along with Jiangxi porcelain, heading towards an unfortunate fate.

It is said that the raw materials for Yixing pottery are only produced in Shushan and Dingshan, Yixing, within China's vast territory. It seems that no other country in the world produces the same fine clay as Yixing. Therefore, until now, no country has been able to imitate Yixing pottery. But now Yixing pottery is declining. It is said that some people are now promoting Jiangxi porcelain and improving it with scientific methods. Why is no one paying attention to this Yixing pottery, which has a long history and is unique in the world?

Finally, I remembered an Yixing friend who once asked me to compose a couplet, with the first line being "Wuxi Yixing clay teapot." The first character of the two place names were both transformed into verbs, very naturally, but I have thought about it for many years and have not been able to come up with a second line. Today, talking about Yixing pottery, I add this as a side note for amusement.

Little Western Heaven 204

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Episode Twenty-Two: Heroic Words Move Rosy Lips, Beauties Gather to Discuss; False Feelings Surprise Jade Wrists, Suffering Woman Escapes Captivity

Everyone in this universe seems to have two faces, one face for competing for fame, and one face for competing for profit. When these two faces are brought out at the same time, they often create great conflicts. The wife of the teacher next door to Cheng Zhiqian was the kind of person who brought out both faces at the same time. Wang Beihai listened blankly for a while, but couldn't help but feel anger rising in his heart, wishing he could jump over to the other room and slap the woman twice. Zhiqian smiled as he looked at his red face and didn't say anything. After a while, that Sister-in-law Hu came out of the room next door, seeming to be walking by with a smile on her face. Beihai really couldn't bear it any longer and, without informing Zhiqian first, got up and walked out. He went straight to the back courtyard entrance and blocked the passageway. Sister-in-law Hu was very familiar with his face, so she stopped and gave him a smile. Beihai's face was still red, and he calmed his breathing before smiling at Sister-in-law Hu: Sister-in-law, you can get another matchmaker's fee. Sister-in-law Hu took two steps back, leaned on the wall, and looked at him with a slight bite on her lip. She smiled and said: Listening to your husband speak, he's also a local. Am I that kind of person? Can't you tell? Beihai put both hands in his trouser pockets, then took them out again, rubbing them together a few times, and then smiled and said: How could I not know what kind of fire you are? I want to say something you won't like to hear: if it's your own relatives, you reluctantly introduce them to be sold, then what daughters of other people can you not introduce? Sister-in-law Hu was stunned by his words and couldn't say anything. Beihai saw that she was silent, so he glared at her and said: Let me tell you. Back when people were starving to death in Xi'an, the government didn't even allow people to be sold. Those who were sold went out secretly to escape for their lives. Now that the place is much more peaceful, poor people can find food to eat, as long as they're not lazy, there's always a way. If you continue to do this bone-selling business, I will definitely report you to the police. (373)

Small Literature and Art

A Big Business with Small Capital 205

— Tian Xu Wo Sheng

Since this newspaper's National Goods Weekly published an article on rice straw papermaking, the number of letters received has been overwhelming. As for newspapers, there is already a government-business joint venture, the China Paper Manufacturing Company, dedicated to making them, and they will soon appear on the market. Our machines are too small and the capital is too large, so we don't need to bother with it. However, improving coarse paper is really a great path. In rural areas, specializing in pulp making can increase production by six times, which is definitely possible. However, selling to paper mills requires credit, and there is neither confidence nor strength, which is a problem. Therefore, I thought of the rice milling plant method. The pulp made in the rural areas can use our existing machines to help everyone make "improved coarse paper" to sell, which is easier to achieve success. There are 450 million people in China, and only those in swaddling clothes don't need paper. Whether male or female, old or young, rich or poor, it can be said that no one doesn't need paper every day. It's just a pity that hand-copied paper is too uneconomical because it consumes time, and the invested capital is not easily turned over, so the value is expensive and cannot compete with machine-made paper. Even in terms of coarse paper, the recent trend has been to use flushing water barrels. Residents in Shanghai and Qingdao have abandoned domestic coarse paper and switched to roll-type pit paper. However, because the price is not cheap, each roll can only be equivalent to one hundred sheets, costing more than ten cents. Therefore, the Hongkou pawnshops sell a kind of gray pit paper. It is made of oil paper, and the cost is half as cheap, so in the near future, Fuyang grass paper will undoubtedly be eliminated. The pit paper produced in Jiangxi, called Zhengxi, is even more expensive than Fuyang grass paper. How can it compete? Therefore, we must hurry up and improve it. It is impossible to switch to machine-made paper everywhere in the interior in a short time. Instead of just talking about it, it is better for everyone to take action and use a cooperative approach, which is easy and both parties can be bold without worry. Therefore, the simple methods are set as follows:

(1) All self-made pulp, whether it is rice straw or wheat straw pulp, or tree bark wood pulp, or ordinary bamboo pulp, does not need to be bleached or made into paper. Just soak it and dry it, making it into something like soybean cakes (in fact, it doesn't need to be dry, but the shipping cost will increase, which may not be cost-effective), and it can be sent to our factory for machine processing to make paper. The easiest to turn into money is "improved coarse paper." Each ton of material can be used to make eighty bundles of "Zhengxi" style pit paper (each bundle has twenty-two reams, and each ream has one hundred and ten sheets), with a labor cost of thirty-six yuan plus four yuan for miscellaneous expenses. Two years ago, the market price of "Zhengxi" was two yuan and six cents per piece. Because there is gray pit paper that is cheaper than it, the price has gradually fallen. Now it has fallen to one yuan and two cents per piece. Even the smaller "Xiaoxi" also sells for one yuan and one cent per piece. It is made by hand, one sheet at a time, and it is simply impossible to earn enough for food. (To be continued)

Street Cigarette Factory 206

— (Qiao Yun Tun)

One day, I went for a walk in Jiangwan Town, and suddenly I discovered this miracle of a street cigarette factory. At first, I thought their raw materials must be those "cigarette butt picking" experts, who were their skirmish line-style tenants; (Note: Manufacturers send staff to various ports to buy raw materials, which is called "going out to the tenants.") After an interview, I found that they were a cut above. I also learned that these street cigarette factories take Jiangwan Town as their headquarters, calling it the main camp. They also have a machine, in the form of a fortune-telling stall. The machine, leaves, and cigarette paper are all sold by the cigarette shop. It is said that most of these cigarette shops are located in the Tangshan Road area of Hongkou. The stall is run by a man or a woman, but only by one person, so the title of "General Manager" is truly well-deserved. The engineer, manager, accountant, shop assistant, etc., can be called a "multifaceted individual." They mix the tobacco leaves, make the cigarettes, collect the payment from customers, and deliver the goods. When they encounter regular customers, they also give gifts. Buy a pack of cigarettes and get one cigarette free. They even exchange a few words of greeting: "Are you busy with your life?" "Is your business good?" With these two sentences, they really use their hands, mouth, ears, and eyes at the same time. They move the factory to the corner of the wall on hot days and to the sunny side on cold days. They say that they can produce hundreds of packs of cigarettes every day, half for retail and half for wholesale. The constant working capital is only three legal tender notes of one yuan each, which is more than enough.

Discussion on Blood Transfusion 208

— Saeki Shigeharu, translated by Zong Ze

Safe Operation Without Danger

—Blood is Still Effective After 25 Days of Storage—

Wide Range of Applications

The so-called blood transfusion is the act of taking as much blood as possible from the body of the blood donor, within the limit of the blood's ability to maintain its full function, and then transferring it to the blood vessels of the person who needs the blood, the recipient. This transfer of blood cannot be performed arbitrarily between people. If incompatible blood is transferred between them, the recipient often risks losing their life. Therefore, blood compatibility is very important in blood transfusion.

Blood Types: Blood can be broadly divided into two types: blood cells (formed components) and blood serum (liquid components). However, now most people separate blood cells and blood serum for observation. For example, if the blood cells of person A are mixed with the blood serum of person B, and the blood serum of person A is mixed with the blood cells of person B, then the phenomenon of agglutination reaction only occurs in the former and not in the latter. If the blood of another two people, B and C, are mixed, the reaction phenomenon does not occur in the former but occurs in the latter. If A and C are mixed, both reactions occur. If C and D are mixed, neither reaction occurs. The agglutination reaction phenomenon varies from person to person. More than ten years ago, several scholars, as a result of examining the agglutination reaction of many people, determined that human blood can be classified into four blood types. The names of these four blood types are O type, A type, B type, and AB type. Among them, even if the blood of people with the same type is mixed, no agglutination reaction occurs. Transfusing blood between people with the same blood type that does not cause a reaction will not cause any danger, as has been clearly understood through various experiences. It is now known that while blood of the same type is suitable for transfusion, it has also been found that transfusing blood between different types is not harmful, and it is also theoretically accepted that blood of type O can be transfused to people of other blood types (A, B, AB), and blood of type AB can also be transfused to people of other blood types (A, B, C).

Blood Donors: In addition to blood compatibility, the necessary condition for blood donors is that they be healthy. Blood that can cause viral infections due to blood transfusions is of course unacceptable. The most effective and appropriate blood is that of healthy and energetic adults. It is also best to avoid any impact on the blood donor during blood collection. Because the blood donor must have a large amount of blood taken, if the blood donor's blood pressure is very high, performing blood collection is not only harmless to the body, but can also eliminate its special state. Performing blood collection on weak and anemic people is very dangerous. From numerous experiences and experiments, it is known that a healthy person can have no more than 10 grams of blood taken per kilogram of body weight. If the body weight is 50 kilograms (about 13 catties), no more than 500 grams of blood can be taken. In this way, even continuous blood collection once a month will not harm the blood donor's body. Generally, the amount of blood required for blood transfusion ranges from 100 grams to 300 grams (up to 500 grams).

Purpose of Blood Transfusion: What kinds of diseases is this blood transfusion method applicable to? When we encounter injuries, duodenal ulcers, pulmonary tuberculosis, hemorrhoids, childbirth, ectopic pregnancy, etc., resulting in the patient having a large hemorrhage and facing a life-threatening situation, the first thing needed is blood supplementation. This is something that everyone can think of. Because after a sudden massive hemorrhage, the blood pressure drops sharply, and this drop in blood pressure can threaten the patient's own life. Therefore, before using surgery or focusing on hemostasis methods and planning other methods, the most important thing is to increase the patient's blood pressure. For this purpose, blood transfusion can be said to be the best method. Secondly, for anemia after massive hemorrhage, duodenal ulcers, stomach cancer, intestinal cancer, uterine cancer, uterine fibroids, hemorrhoids, pulmonary tuberculosis and other diseases, anemia caused by chronic bleeding, as well as infectious diseases, parasitic diseases, and various drug poisoning caused by toxins, as well as other types of anemia, and to thicken the blood in those with thin blood, blood transfusion methods can be used. In the case of chronic bleeding, it also has the meaning of hemostasis.

The blood that has been injected into the body has the effect of stimulating hematopoietic organs and promoting blood regeneration. For example, in patients with stomach cancer, judging from the course of the disease, removing the cancer is the radical cure. However, if the patient's physical strength is weak and they cannot undergo strong surgery, we usually use several blood transfusions to increase the patient's physical strength, and then perform major surgery to achieve the goal of curing the cancer. In addition, patients with hemophilia who bleed because their blood lacks coagulability and is temporarily difficult to stop, can also achieve considerable results if they frequently undergo blood transfusions, because the blood of healthy people contains the necessary substances for coagulating blood.

Blood transfusion can also be applied to acute infectious diseases such as sepsis, acute peritonitis, acute osteomyelitis, cellulitis, erysipelas, intestinal typhus, dysentery, etc., because these diseases are caused by toxins destroying a large number of red blood cells in the human body. By using blood transfusion methods, the deficiency of red blood cells can be supplemented, and at the same time, toxins existing in the body can be destroyed and the number of bacteria in the blood can be reduced. A method that further enhances its effectiveness for the purpose of antitoxin and antibacterial is called immune blood transfusion. For example, by adopting the blood of patients in the recovery period who have the same disease course as the patient for blood transfusion, or by proactively administering immunization injections to the blood donor, their immunity can be increased, because the blood of people in the recovery period contains a large amount of immune substances. In addition, blood transfusion can also be effective for burns, eclampsia, carbuncle, carbon gas poisoning, mushroom poisoning, and various other drug poisonings. When dealing with patients with infectious diseases or poisoning, they can first have blood let (blood must be prepared in advance), and then administer blood transfusion, which is even more effective - and on the other hand, we want to talk about the danger of blood transfusion.

Side Effects of Blood Transfusion: If the selection of blood is not wrong and the blood transfusion method is proper, death directly caused by blood transfusion can be said to be extremely rare. However, it cannot be said that there are no side effects at all. Including the very mild ones, about 20% of people experience some kind of side effect. Lighter symptoms include fatigue, chills, hot flashes, fever, headache, palpitations, dizziness, urticaria.

Page 17

rash, mild abdominal pain, etc. Severe symptoms include chills, shivering, high fever, nausea, vomiting, severe back pain, abdominal pain, diarrhea, difficulty breathing, poor pulse, delirium, etc. Although such situations may cause extreme panic among the people around, most of them are temporary phenomena. After twelve hours (at most several hours), the patient can return to their previous state. Although the cause of these side effects has been clarified after much research, even if there are no shortcomings in the operation, such situations often occur, and encountering such situations to a certain degree is dangerous. Therefore, blood transfusion is not something that anyone can perform. It must be implemented after careful consideration of each individual's situation.

Blood Transfusion Methods: There are two methods of blood transfusion: (1) Directly transfusing the collected blood to the recipient without adding any substances—direct method. (2) Adding citric acid soda to the collected blood to remove its blood clotting properties before infusing it—indirect method. If a suitable blood is found for the direct method, it is theoretically very appropriate to deliver it to the recipient in its original composition, and in practice, there are very few side effects. However, due to various operational inconveniences, it is not widely used. The indirect method is more successful because it can prevent blood clotting, and its effect is not much different from the direct method. Therefore, most people currently use this method. In addition, blood with citric acid soda can be stored in a refrigerator for about ten periods, and it is possible to transport it to a distant place for blood transfusion. Regarding the storage period of blood, blood stored for up to 25 days still has considerable effect. This is the result of recent research.

Furthermore, if the blood is once turned into dry powder, it can be dissolved into a liquid before use and then infused. This is the so-called dry blood transfusion method. Although this is slightly different from the true meaning of blood transfusion, it can at least achieve part of the purpose of blood transfusion.

Common Knowledge Questions and Answers on Diseases 209

— Cheng Hanzhang

(Question) What is schistosomiasis?

(Answer) This is a disease caused by a type of fluke that parasitizes in the blood vessels of the portal vein of the human liver. It is specifically called Japanese schistosomiasis because it was prevalent in several places in Japan. Recently, this parasitic disease has also been found in several places in our country.

(Question) How do these flukes invade the human body?

(Answer) They penetrate the human body through the skin or are ingested through drinking water.

(Question) Where do blood flukes parasitize before invading the human body?

(Answer) Their intermediate host is a type of snail.

(Question) How big are blood flukes?

(Answer) Male worms are about 15 to 16 millimeters long (equivalent to 0.4 to 0.5 inches), and female worms are about 19 to 21 millimeters long (equivalent to 0.6 to 0.7 inches), but the female worms are much thinner than the male worms.

(Question) What effects do blood flukes have on the organs of a person with schistosomiasis?

(Answer) The human organ directly affected is the liver. The liver initially swells and then shrinks and hardens. The surface develops small hill-like protrusions and depressions. Sometimes, because the worm eggs travel through the large veins to the lungs, the lungs also undergo the same changes as the liver. Other organs, such as the spleen, also swell, and the mucous membranes of the large and small intestines become inflamed and swollen, or develop small ulcers.

(Question) What are the symptoms of a person with schistosomiasis?

(Answer) There are two types of symptoms of schistosomiasis: acute and chronic.

(Question) What are the symptoms of the acute type?

(Answer) There is localized itchy dermatitis, especially common in the lower limbs. About two weeks after infection, initial symptoms include general fatigue, loss of appetite, and abdominal pain; after three weeks, due to the worms laying eggs in the portal vein branches of the intestinal wall, acute enteritis or appendicitis-like symptoms develop, sometimes with fever and liver swelling.

(Question) What are the symptoms of the chronic type?

(Answer) Some develop from repeated acute attacks, while others are chronic from the beginning. The liver gradually swells and hardens, becoming tender to the touch. As the disease progresses, the liver shrinks, and various sizes of granules can be felt on its surface. At the same time, there are symptoms such as anemia and digestive disorders, stomach pain, abdominal distension, palpitations, and difficulty breathing, sometimes with edema, ascites, or jaundice, and gastrointestinal bleeding.

(Question) How can a diagnosis be made to confirm schistosomiasis?

(Answer) If liver enlargement, mucosal bleeding, and portal vein congestion are encountered in an endemic area, this disease can be considered. It is even more certain to prove the presence of worm eggs in the stool.

(Question) Which diseases should it be distinguished from?

(Answer) It should be distinguished from Banti's disease and Laennec's cirrhosis.

Common Knowledge Questions and Answers on Teeth (12) 210

— Lin Jianxian

(Question 66) How many types of systemic contributing factors are there?

(Answer) Systemic contributing factors can be divided into two categories: congenital and acquired. Congenital factors are related to heredity and are beyond one's control. For example, if parents are physically weak, have low resistance, or have unhealthy teeth, their children's teeth will also be weak, have no resistance, and be very prone to cavities. Acquired factors can be said to include any lifestyle abnormality that can reduce the body's resistance, which can induce cavities. In particular, the following reasons are even more significant: (1) Nutritional disorders, physical weakness, leading to decalcification. (2) Insufficient nutrients in the diet, lack of phosphorus, calcium, vitamins, etc. (3) Suffering from lung disease, venereal disease, typhoid fever, metabolic diseases such as diabetes, etc. (4) Saliva changes, losing its alkalinity, unable to neutralize lactic acid and prevent the development of bacteria. (5) Loss of calcium during pregnancy.

(Question 67) Which part of the tooth is most prone to cavities?

(Answer) Any concave area on the surface of the tooth, and areas where the enamel is incompletely developed, such as the grooves on the occlusal surface of molars, and concave lines and small pits on other surfaces, are most prone to cavities. Also, the gaps between two adjacent teeth, and the area around the neck of the tooth near the gums, are also very prone to cavities; because these areas are not easily reached by friction, brushing is difficult, and food is most likely to linger. Also, upper incisors are more prone to cavities than lower incisors. This is because the lower incisors are located where the sublingual glands secrete, and can receive more protection from saliva.

(Question 68) How do cavities progress?

(Answer) The surface of the enamel, where it is eroded by lactic acid, dissolves the colloid, first becoming rough. The erosion gradually deepens, forming small holes. Then food and bacteria are more likely to stay, and the erosion is faster. When the cavity penetrates the enamel and reaches the dentin, it is like breaking a bamboo. This is because the dentin softens when it encounters acid, and the softened dentin allows bacteria to penetrate, fermenting inside the dentin and encountering the action of acid. Bacteria and acid collude, so the erosion is extremely fast, eventually penetrating the pulp chamber and killing the dental pulp.

(Question 69) When does tooth decay cause pain?

(Answer) When the decay reaches the dentin, there will be a feeling of soreness. Especially when stimulated by cold, heat, or acidic substances. When the decay is close to the dental pulp, severe pain often occurs.

(Question 70) What pulp diseases can cavities cause?

(Answer) The earliest is pulp hyperemia, then pulpitis, and finally pulp necrosis.

(Question) What is the degree of danger of this disease?

(Answer) The acute type is mostly good, and it can be completely cured after a few weeks to two or three months. The chronic type can last for twenty or thirty years, and death occurs due to general weakness.

(Question) How to treat it?

(Answer) Only administering a combination of quinine and tartar emetic or injecting Salvarsan.

Common Knowledge of Ear, Nose, Throat and Eye Hygiene 211

— Tang Renjin

(72) Foreign Objects in the Nose

Foreign objects in the nose are common, especially in young children. Clinically, it is often encountered. Now I will briefly talk about the types of foreign objects and the symptoms they cause. Types of foreign objects = Young children mostly use slate pencils, chalk, and erasers, or play with buttons, chess pieces, and beans. Therefore, the types of foreign objects mostly belong to these types. The chance of foreign objects entering is usually due to automatic insertion into the nose. Rarely passive intrusion.

Symptoms caused by foreign objects = After a foreign object is inserted into the nose, if it can be discovered immediately and taken out by a doctor, no symptoms should occur. If it is not discovered and taken out after a day or two, the nasal cavity will suddenly overflow with nasal fluid. The nasal fluid is initially a thin mucus: then it becomes purulent and has an odor. At the same time, the nasal cavity feels blocked (if the foreign object is a bean, it can swell when it encounters nasal fluid, and the nasal obstruction will also increase accordingly). At this time, the parents of the child often think that the child has a nasal tumor or cerebrospinal fluid leak. The child often forgets the process of inserting the foreign object. Only after the doctor's examination can the existence of the foreign object be discovered. Facts of this kind are often encountered clinically. The author recently encountered a case. It was a five-year-old boy. His symptom was that the bridge of his nose was particularly swollen. A yellowish-green purulent secretion flowed out of his nose. The nasal cavity on the affected side was completely blocked. This situation lasted for about four months. The parents thought that the child had a tumor in the nasal cavity. However, the examination revealed a small piece of green eraser. The outside of the eraser was stained with purulent secretions. The mucous membrane of the nasal cavity was also swollen and eroded. Therefore, as parents, if you encounter a child with unilateral nasal obstruction and nasal discharge, you should immediately pay attention to whether there is a foreign object in the child's nose. If there is any doubt, you should immediately seek medical attention to examine the nasal cavity. It should not be difficult to solve.

Also, when there is a foreign object in the nose, families often try to remove it themselves. If the method is not appropriate, it is easy to push it into the back of the nasal cavity, which causes fear, thinking that it can invade the brain. In fact, foreign objects can pass from the back of the nasal cavity, through the nasopharynx, and reach the oral cavity. So, there is no need to panic.

The treatment method for foreign objects in the nose is to determine the foreign object and then use appropriate instruments to remove it, and it will be cured.

Knowledge Robbers 212

— Jia Wei

Every day when I open the local news, "abduction," "seduction," "abandonment"... such scandals and troubles occur several times a day. And the statistics of weekly criminal events of university students committing fraud and becoming thieves, and even municipal authorities and the Public Works Department, etc.: cases of stealing, theft, kidnapping, and robbery are increasing rather than decreasing, which tells us about the social pathology of today—can't you see it? The recent news that the Jiangsu No. 2 Prison in Caohejing is overcrowded and will carry out a large-scale parole of old prisoners of up to six or seven hundred people is a very real reflection!

The news also reported that a young robber who had received higher education was sentenced to ten years in prison. It is said that this young man is proficient in several languages and has received higher education. He is from Shandong Province, 24 years old. He was sentenced to six years in prison for carrying weapons and robbing in a group of three or more people, seven years in prison for attempted murder, and seven years of deprivation of political rights. He should serve ten years in prison and seven years of deprivation of political rights.

It seems rare to hear about this kind of "knowledge robber" who is proficient in several languages and has received higher education, right? I remember a few months ago, when a college student became a thief, it attracted the attention of the general public and the media, and a review of the employment, unemployment, and even the entire future of young people was made. But here, I don't know what else to say?

Originally, "the future of young people" is not a simple problem, and the fact that "intellectuals" want to commit robbery is not accidental. Everyone can see it, right? In recent years, with the social depression—rural bankruptcy, market depression, economic depression in all industries—the general working people are struggling in the face of hunger and death under heavy oppression, and the general petty bourgeoisie is also inevitably declining; at the same time, a large number of "intellectuals" are unable to find a way out and are down and out... all of these are undeniable facts.

However, the fact that "intellectuals" commit theft is not just starting today. The smuggling of antiques by a certain important person, the private sale of public power by a certain politician, and the bribery and secret plunder of corrupt officials have all become open secrets.

Originally, our society has been evolving in such a complex and chaotic way. How should we see through and recognize these facts and make effective preparations!

Untitled (and Another One) 213

— Liang Qiyun

Untitled

Under the lamp, listening to the autumn wind gently tapping the window with raindrops, sometimes slow, sometimes fast, the bleak autumn feeling can't bear the loneliness and is sobbing. The past is surging in my heart like a tide.

But, the past can only add to sorrow. The more I think, the more chaotic it becomes. I want to cut it off, but I can't...

Yes, what I fear most when I am idle is thinking about the past. I don't know why, the old memories are always so beautiful, but the situation in front of me is always

Page 19

so cursed.

I once compared this old temper to a devil. That guy is terrible! When I'm happy, it disappears without a trace; but when troubles come, it makes me even more dizzy.

I was angry. I used the most cruel words to scold my nerves, questioning why it allowed these ghosts to fight and occupy my brain.

——Be quiet! The sea can't rise waves without wind.

In confusion, it seemed that a soft voice was saying softly.

So, I stood up and turned off the lights.

The night is quiet.

In order to avoid troubles, I closed my eyes, rested my head on the window frame, and silently listened to the sound of rain sobbing in the night wind...

Sending to a Distant Old Friend 214

The small building is immersed in the sound of rain again tonight.

Thinking of you on a distant southern island, I am lost again. It's not because I'm sighing at the rapid passage of days; my friend, think about it, it's really those past memories that are too worthy of nostalgia. At that time, I didn't know what autumn depression was, what winter horror was; I only knew spring, spring, every day was spring.

So, after you left, I began to learn to be silent.

"Learn slowly, from silence, you will understand why life is. Gradually, gradually, you will understand that there is nothing to pursue in the world."

That friend in his thirties who had recently become a widower, one day when he discovered that I was staring at your photo, he said to me affectionately.

The reason I became silent is based on this.

But, whenever I am alone and trapped in boredom, I feel that neither the left nor the right is right, and I will overturn the reason for this silence. ——I am not a lark, why should I lock myself in a cage? Moreover, even if it is a lark, it will not lock itself up.

For this reason, there was a time when I often strolled in the autumn countryside every evening. Therefore, I got used to the curling smoke rising from the distant gardens, and I was also familiar with the melancholy face of the setting sun in the west. Until the twilight dyed the surroundings with a gray color reminiscent of an ancient tomb, I dragged my heavy steps back.

Maybe you will say; "Why so melancholy?" No,... I only hope to have a chance to break this oppressive cage and let the lark fly out freely.

So, I opened the window. Let the cold night wind wake up my confused nerves, let the raindrops gently caress my face, my hair...

Oh, my friend, will spring also, like me, come again after a short period of silence?

"There is no reason why it can't exist."——You might answer like this.

Yes, my friend, it will come. But, you have to remember: "Without you, I have no spring."

Because of this reason, I can't say anything else.

Song of the Eagle (Continued) 215

— Lao Xin

Silence is terrible pain. Occasionally raising our heads, four eyes looking at four eyes: fixed, without light, cracking a bitter smile, and lowering our heads again.

A goshawk swept across the sky, stretching its two powerful wings, flying from here to there, from there to here, flying so majestic and freely. Its head and neck stretched forward, and from its hard beak, it sang a clear and crisp song, like a horn, piercing our ears sharply, piercing our throbbing hearts. We heard a friend's song in our ears:

"I love to see the goshawk flying in the sky, and I love to hear its clear song! Young friends, don't forget: what it tells us!"

Hot blood was boiling, and the four of us jumped up, forgetting the tragedy we had just witnessed. We turned away from the gray color brought by the tragedy, we jumped excitedly, we raised our heads, facing the free and majestic goshawk, we echoed with rough voices, we sang:

"We love to see the goshawk flying in the sky, we love to hear its clear song! We have not forgotten what it tells us!"

We began to fly, learning to fly in the sky like a goshawk, learning to fly like our dear friend. Our boiling hot blood was encouraging ourselves, for our own rights.

The south is a ball of fire, we flew with this flame, from here to there, and from there to there. We are all young, we all have a pair of strong arms and a pair of strong legs, and the goshawk also has a pair of strong wings. We are like eagles, flying like eagles, flying freely: flying to whatever place. We also have a voice, shouting out the clear song roughly, the same song as the goshawk. We love to hear this song, and we also love to sing this song.

So, we forgot the depression, and we also tore down the gray curtain of the tragedy, although it was still the dark night before the sun came out, we were flying so excitedly.—We sang the Song of the Eagle for the first time in a loud voice.

At this time, we remembered our friend who had been separated for a long time, the friend who was flying like an eagle, we silently recited his song, and silently prayed for his health. We were not ashamed, we just used the facts to tell him: we did not forget him for a moment.

Now, it is such a dark night again. A gray curtain covered my eyes again, and I was dropped into the fence of silence again. I raised my head, and in the sky I saw the goshawk flying again, and the clear song boiled my hot blood again. So I straightened my chest, stretched my neck, and sang the Song of the Eagle:

(...We have not forgotten what he told us!)! (End)

A Preference for Green and Blue 216

— Ming Meng

Among all the natural colors, what I love most is green, followed by blue, which is close to green. People's preference for colors is more emotional than rational; it is better to say that it is intuitive than explainable. Therefore, I don't want to explain my preference for green or blue. If I have to say something, it may be based on my love of nature.

In the house, I love green decorations. I love to paste green paper on the walls, love to wrap my cherished books in green paper covers; make green cloth into tablecloths, and also make green cushions into chair cushions. For other utensils, whenever possible, I always like to choose green ones to use. I decorate the house with a green theme, and then sit in it alone, smoking a cigarette leisurely. Whether dreaming, thinking, reading, or writing, I feel warm and harmonious, and my spirit is refreshed. Otherwise, if the room is changed to a red, dark yellow, light gray, or other colorful or dark colors, my spirit will not be able to concentrate, and my nerves will be disturbed.

Lying in a green room at night, the sleepiness is thick and sweet. When I am about to fall asleep, I glimpse the green luster around me, projecting on the corners of my eyes, directly piercing my heart. My heart seems to be ironed, and I feel unusually comfortable, so I can sleep peacefully. When I wake up, open my sleepy eyes, and glimpse the blurred green in the room, I will joyfully rub my eyes, yawn, and climb up happily. It is said that the green color in the bedroom is most suitable for sleep. I don't know the reason, but based on my intuition, I do feel that the gentleness of green is most helpful for sound sleep, and even dreaming is sweet.

Based on my love for green, I love to stand by the window and look out. Watching the green forest in the village and the blue sky is most likely to stimulate my imagination. I often stand by the window for several hours, letting the wings of imagination fly on the green treetops and in the blue sky, until I am immersed in a state of almost ignorance and unconsciousness. Maeterlinck's "The Blue Bird" was particularly loved in my youth. Now that I think about it, the reason seems not accidental, right?

Because I love green, I love to climb high mountains and travel. Because only on high mountains can I see a wider green field; only in travel can I broaden my horizons. I can see the fresh colors of the green fields in different places and smell the fragrance of the green forest. I have climbed quite a few high mountains, although not many. Although the scenery in each place is different, and the tastes are different, the same glimpse of the green forest, the sight of the green field, and the look up at the vast blue sky are equally satisfying. On high mountains, the endless green of the green forest and grass, and the green color of the villages and fields are clear at a glance. As for the vast and distant sky, it cannot be seen by living in a narrow room, right?

From the carriages or ships of travel, you can also see the green fields and plants, and the sky hanging high above the blue river and sea. Trains or pleasure boats, because of long-distance travel, pass through countless mountains, fields, dense forests, and swamps. From here, I can expand my vision as much as possible and capture all the green luster along the way. As for the ship in the sea, the sky and the sea are both a vast blue, at that time, except for the rare white clouds and the rainbow on the horizon, almost all of them are a blue color. Then the sea's love for me is needless to say.

Therefore, I love the ocean more than the land, love the high mountains more than the plains, love the countryside more than the city, love the rivers more than the wilderness, and love the wilderness more than the room. Based on my preference for colors, my temperament and worldview have been completely determined. The influence of colors on me can be said to be very large.

Red is more stimulating, gray is more sentimental, yellow makes people feel turbid, black makes people sad, I still love peaceful and gentle green, and imaginative blue!

Narcissus 217

— Xiao Wen

My father was a man who deeply loved nature, so his fondness for flowers and plants was a given. However, whether his lack of a singular passion made him a step below Tao Yuanming is debatable. Still, he bought narcissus every year. When he did, I felt that the New Year was approaching, because it was only available in winter and was used to decorate homes at the end and beginning of the year. Though narcissus doesn't bloom in a riot of reds and greens, its long green leaves give rise to white petals with yellow hearts, creating a magnificent display that inspires nothing but pure thoughts. When in full bloom, it also emits a faint, elegant fragrance. Paired with white pebbles in an antique pot, it exudes grandeur and spirit. If I had to use two words to describe narcissus, “refined charm” would encompass all its qualities.

When spring was about to sprout, the narcissus would wither. Some suggested hanging the bulbs under the eaves to prevent them from rotting and decaying, saying they would be useful next year, and that dried narcissus, like “three-year-old moxa,” could cure ailments. However, we always discarded them. Once, my brother tried the method, but they didn't grow or bloom. Perhaps his technique was not refined enough, and he never bothered with it again. I've seen my father buy narcissus more than just once or twice. His state of mind changed every year, and changed rapidly. During that time, my father also seemed to age.

There was a time when I didn't see my father for two years. I don't know if he bought narcissus or not. This year, I saw my father bring narcissus home again, but he had added a layer of colorful stones from Nanjing's Yuhuatai on top of the white pebbles, giving it a fresh look. The narcissus was as beautiful as ever, while I was growing older year by year, and my father had aged even more. Why couldn't he have the same spirit as the narcissus every year? I don't know if I will be able to see my father buy narcissus again next year, and see it bloom once more with its white petals and yellow hearts. White pebbles covered with colorful stones from Yuhuatai, paired with an antique pot and placed on a redwood stand, were displayed beneath several painted screens, highlighting the narcissus’s refined charm.

A local superstition says that the prosperity of a family is tied to the flourishing or decline of flowers. At the end of the year, people want everything to be auspicious, so naturally, they would divine the fate of the family based on the state of the narcissus. However, my own observation, albeit based on superstition, suggests otherwise. The two narcissus plants in my home flourished or withered depending on their location. The true needs of narcissus are water and sunlight. A narcissus deprived of water and sunlight will wither and die. Yet, dark clouds often obscure the sun. If we are also receiving the blessings of water and sunlight, then we, too, should have the same spirit as the narcissus.

In a north-facing room, there is a pot of narcissus, suffering the unfortunate fate of not being touched by sunlight. Gradually, it withered and turned yellow. Thinking of my own situation, I should put that pot of narcissus in the sun so it can be free from the suffering of neglect and burst forth with a few charming blooms.

Because of Mr. Xie's death, it is heard that the bureau has now hired Mr. Zhou Jiaoqing to teach, still broadcasting on the China West Radio Station (1040 rate) every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday, starting at 7:00 AM. The teaching materials used are Progressive English China Weekly, supplemented by practical selections such as basic conversational vocational English. The teaching is earnest and easy to understand. English pronunciation is still taught by Mr. Zhou on the Li Shude Tang Radio Station (940) starting at 6:30 AM. Mr. Zhou is an English expert, and is also proficient in French, German, Italian, Japanese, Russian, and other languages. He has stayed in England and the United States for many years, and strongly advocates education. His teaching of English is rich in experience, his pronunciation is correct, he is not拘束 at all, his lectures are earnest, his analysis is clear and detailed, and he explains everything without reservation, so that listeners are enlightened. Now, he teaches every morning through radio waves, which is truly gospel for those who want to learn English. Those who are interested, please pay attention.

Movie News

"Peach Blossom Dream" to be Released Soon 224

"Peach Blossom Dream" is the first great product of Dan Duyu after changing his style. It took eight months of filming to complete. The play contains two major parts: the natural beauty of the countryside and the prosperity of the city. The actions of the characters in the play also change with the environment. Those who are not naturally talented in art cannot fulfill this role well. Led by Yin Mingzhu, the remaining cast members such as Cang Yin, Qiu Lei, Meng Na, as well as singers and dancers such as Xu Can Ying and Bao Xi Xi, all have profound performances. Those who have seen its preview say that the scene can be compared to "A Poet's Journey to Hell", and the skill surpasses it. It will be released at the Jin Cheng Grand Theater in this city soon, and movie fans will surely be eager to see it first.

"National Defense Great Secret" 225

Sets New Sales Record in America

"The Count of Monte Cristo" starring Robert Donat, and Marlene Carroll, the female lead in "Scarlet Empress" and "The Hated Wife of King Henry", co-star in "The 39 Steps". When the film was released at the Roxy Theatre in New York, the sales were so high that it broke the "earth-shattering" sales record that had not been broken for six years. The entire American film industry was shaken, and it was praised as Britain's unprecedented world masterpiece. The content of the film, whether in terms of plot, performance, or photography, is indeed outstanding in every aspect. This film has already arrived in Shanghai, and it is said that it will soon be released at the Great Light Cinema. This is indeed a piece of news worth reporting to all Shanghai movie fans.

About Flower of Spring 226

Wu Cun's works often have a subtle sense of humor, which is amusing without being over the top. He can express the essence of a tragedy with comedic techniques, making the audience often let out a humorous wry smile in a helplessly depressing environment. In his new work "Flower of Spring", in addition to the usual urban night scenes, snowy streets, flowing ice rivers, palace-style dance halls, and other beautiful scenes, the insertions of film company productions, military camp life, and so on, are all in a relaxed tone. In the witty dialogue, a kind of meaning that makes people smile knowingly is conveyed in a roundabout way. Recently, the interior scenes are being actively filmed, and in the near future, he will be traveling to the northern country to shoot exterior scenes!

Silver Miscellaneous Notes 227

— Zhi Er

Shakespeare's "A Midsummer Night's Dream" truly makes people feel like they have had a wonderful dream after watching it. Of course, its social value now is just like a "dream".

After watching "A Midsummer Night's Dream", I have a few thoughts: First, the progress of photography techniques, like smoke and dreams, is extremely beautiful; second, the compactness of the scene transitions and the director's agility in technique. Especially the second point makes people believe that with a good script (just talking about the production) and a good director, even without good actors, the play will not fail.

"A Midsummer Night's Dream" will be screened at the Great Light after the Cathay, and the seat prices will not increase.

"Hero of the Times" had a public preview at the Jin Cheng Grand Theater yesterday. According to those who have seen it, Shang Guan Wu's acting is indeed very good.

"Camera" writes: After calculating, only Ren Gong Jin Ping can be called a "hero of the times" in the film industry. If not for the "situation" of Rehua... how could there be this "hero" Ren Gong.

"King of Blockbusters" Tianlun has the advertisement of "International Premiere" at the Great Light in yesterday's Shen Bao, but there is no date because the Great Light has not scheduled it yet. The screening period is two days.

Lianhua and Jincheng signed a contract, so Jincheng sued the court, and Jincheng lost the case. It is said that in the contract, Lianhua gives Jincheng twenty-four films every year, including six blockbusters, and two of them can be given to the Great Light for screening. Lianhua only produced six films this year, and Tianlun was one of them, going to the Great Light. Jincheng's reason is like this.

It is also rumored that Tianlun was originally scheduled to be released at the Jincheng on Double Ten Festival, but was taken away by the electric power's urban scenery. Jincheng borrowed three thousand gold from Lianhua, and negotiated to schedule Tianlun for the next holiday.

Now I don't know if "International Premiere" will be followed by a continued screening at Jincheng?
